The Step() method implements the exponential backoff calculation.\\n\\n4. **delay Function (line 98)**: Core algorithm that calculates the next delay interval. with automatic reset after a specified duration.\\n\\nAlternatively, Kubernetes also maintains a separate exponential backoff implementation in backoff directly: starting with minDelay, doubling on each failure (up to maxDelay), and stopping at maxRetries or function completion.\\n\\n4. **Provisioning Resource Retry Queue Manager (storage/remote/queue_manager.go, line 2022)**: The `sendWriteRequestWithBackoff()` function retries write requests with exponential backoff. It starts with MinBackoff from config, doubles on retry, respects Retry-After headers, and caps at MaxBackoff (default 5 seconds). Failure to send samples triggers backoff and disables resharding to avoid amplifying rate limiting.\\n\\n2. **Configuration (config/config.go, line 1561)**: Remote write config defines MinBackoff (default 30ms) and MaxBackoff (default 5 seconds) parameters used for exponential backoff calculation.\\n\\n3. **TSDB Compaction (tsdb/db.go, line 2606)**: The `exponential()` function implements a simple exponential backoff by doubling duration each call, bounded by minD and maxD. Used in the compaction retry loop to back off between failed compaction attempts (lines 1231-1234).\\n\\n4. **Remote Write Client (storage/remote/client.go)**: Handles backoff-related errors with support for Retry-After headers from servers.\\n\\n## Key Patterns\\n\\nAll three implementations share common characteristics:\\n- **Doubling Strategy**: Duration is multiplied by a factor (typically 2.0) on each retry\\n- **Bounded Growth**: Maximum delay caps exponential growth to prevent excessive waits\\n- **Jitter**: Random variance prevents thundering herd problems when multiple clients retry simultaneously\\n- **Attempt Limits**: Configured maximum attempt counts prevent infinite retry loops\\n- **Configurable Delays**: Initial, maximum, and multiplier values are all tunable per use case\\n\\nThe implementations differ in their deployment:\\n- Kubernetes provides a reusable wait package used by most Go applications on K8s\\n- Grafana uses both the Kubernetes package and external libraries (nanogit, cenkalti/backoff)\\n- Prometheus implements its own backoff for remote write while delegating compaction backoff to simple exponential growth\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2314,"cache_read_input_tokens":74846,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2314},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"feb08f5d-7c12-48df-b2d1-79ed1e7beb89","uuid":"fcf7dc57-a2f6-4575-8071-6b31ea636855"}

cenkalti/backoff/v4 library, providing exponential backoff for alert scheduling.\\n\\n3. **Utility Retryer (pkg/util/retryer/retryer.go, line 18)**: The `Retry()` function implements exponential backoff directly: starting with minDelay, doubling on each failure (up to maxDelay), and stopping at maxRetries or function completion.\\n\\n4. **Provisioning Resource Retry (pkg/registry/apis/provisioning/resources/retry_client.go, line 43)**: The `defaultRetryBackoff()` function uses the Kubernetes wait.Backoff struct with 100ms initial duration, 2.0 factor, 0.1 jitter, and 8 steps capped at 5 seconds.\\n\\n### Prometheus (prometheus/prometheus)\\n\\nPrometheus implements exponential backoff for remote write operations and TSDB compaction:\\n\\n1. **Remote Write Queue Manager (storage/remote/queue_manager.go, line 2022)**: The `sendWriteRequestWithBackoff()` function retries write requests with exponential backoff. It starts with MinBackoff from config, doubles on retry, respects Retry-After headers, and caps at MaxBackoff (default 5 seconds). Failure to send samples triggers backoff and disables resharding to avoid amplifying rate limiting.\\n\\n2. **Configuration (config/config.go, line 1561)**: Remote write config defines MinBackoff (default 30ms) and MaxBackoff (default 5 seconds) parameters used for exponential backoff calculation.\\n\\n3. **TSDB Compaction (tsdb/db.go, line 2606)**: The `exponential()` function implements a simple exponential backoff by doubling duration each call, bounded by minD and maxD. Used in the compaction retry loop to back off between failed compaction attempts (lines 1231-1234).\\n\\n4. **Remote Write Client (storage/remote/client.go)**: Handles backoff-related errors with support for Retry-After headers from servers.\\n\\n## Key Patterns\\n\\nAll three implementations share common characteristics:\\n- **Doubling Strategy**: Duration is multiplied by a factor (typically 2.0) on each retry\\n- **Bounded Growth**: Maximum delay caps exponential growth to prevent excessive waits\\n- **Jitter**: Random variance prevents thundering herd problems when multiple clients retry simultaneously\\n- **Attempt Limits**: Configured maximum attempt counts prevent infinite retry loops\\n- **Configurable Delays**: Initial, maximum, and multiplier values are all tunable per use case\\n\\nThe implementations differ in their deployment:\\n- Kubernetes provides a reusable wait package used by most Go applications on K8s\\n- Grafana uses both the Kubernetes package and external libraries (nanogit, cenkalti/backoff)\\n- Prometheus implements its own backoff for remote write while delegating compaction backoff to simple exponential growth\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
